## 🔍 Cross-Page Patterns: Common HTML Issues

These HTML patterns cause the same accessibility errors across multiple pages. **Fix the pattern once in your codebase to fix it everywhere!**

### 🎯 Top Patterns to Fix (Highest Impact)

#### Pattern 1: Affects 114 page(s) - 114 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: axe
**Rule**: [landmark-unique](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/landmark-unique?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate
**Issue**: Landmarks should have a unique role or role/label/title (i.e. accessible name) combination

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<nav class="navbar navbar-expand-md navbar-dark navbar-top-vp w-100">
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
#block-headerblock > .navbar-expand-md.navbar-top-vp.navbar-dark
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('#block-headerblock > .navbar-expand-md.navbar-top-vp.navbar-dark')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://valitsus.ee/
- https://valitsus.ee/ru/search?filters%5Btype%5D=%D0%9D%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%BE%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B8&amp;filters%5Bkeyword%5D=
- https://valitsus.ee/ru/search?search_term=&amp;f%5B0%5D=type%3Anews
- https://valitsus.ee/en
- https://valitsus.ee/juurdepaasetavus
- *...and 109 more page(s)*

#### Pattern 2: Affects 97 page(s) - 97 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**Issue**: Target has insufficient size

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<a class="list-group-item list-group-item-action" href="https://riigikantselei.ee/asutus-uudised-ja-kontakt/isikuandmete-tootlemine#cookies" rel="noopener" style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); font-size: 1rem; text-align: left; display: inline !important;" target="_blank">...</a>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/a[@class="list-group-item list-group-item-action"]
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/a[@class="list-group-item list-group-item-action"]')`

#### Pattern 3: Affects 67 page(s) - 134 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)
**Issue**: The element does not have a unique ID

**HTML Pattern**:
```html

            </a>
```

**Scanner**: axe
**Rule**: [aria-allowed-attr](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-allowed-attr?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical
**Issue**: Elements must only use supported ARIA attributes

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<span class="nav-link dropdown-toggle is-active" id="header-language-dropdown" data-toggle="dropdown" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false" tabindex="0">

      </span>
```

#### Pattern 15: Affects 65 page(s) - 65 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: axe
**Rule**: [region](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/region?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate
**Issue**: All page content should be contained by landmarks

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<a href="#main-content" class="visually-hidden focusable skip-link">
      Liigu edasi põhisisu juurde
    </a>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
.focusable
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('.focusable')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:

## Detailed Failure Information (ALFA)

### https://valitsus.ee/

#### Rule: [SIA-R11: Button elements have an accessible name](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r11)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The link does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<a href="https://www.youtube.com/@ValitsuseUudised/streams" target="_blank" rel="noopener">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button type="button" class="eu-cookie-compliance-select-categories-button btn btn-outline-light btn-sm mr-2" tabindex="0">Valin ise</button>`

- XPath: `/button[@class="agree-button btn btn-sm btn-primary mb-sm-0 mr-sm-1"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="nav-link external-link-vp text-white" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#accessibility-modal" href="#accessibility-modal" aria-label="Juurdepääsetavus">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="nav-link external-link-vp text-white"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="https://www.eesti.ee/et" target="_blank" class="nav-link" rel="noopener">Eesti.ee</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="nav-link"]`

*... and 6 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R18: ARIA states are consistent with element semantics](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r18)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is prohibited for the element on which it is specified

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID

- XPath: `/a[@id="header-menu-dropdown"]`

- XPath: `/h4`

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Some `navigation` have the same name.

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 5.39:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R77](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r77)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The cell is not assigned to any header cell
- HTML: `<td class=" text-center no-wrap-vp doc-item-url">...</td>`
- XPath: `/td[@class=" text-center no-wrap-vp doc-item-url"]`

- Message: The first tabbable element in the document is not a semantic link

- HTML: `<button type="button" class="agree-necessary btn btn-outline-light btn-sm mr-2" tabindex="0">Разрешить необходимые</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="agree-necessary btn btn-outline-light btn-sm mr-2"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button type="button" class="agree-button btn btn-sm btn-primary mb-sm-0 mr-sm-1" tabindex="0">Разрешить все</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="agree-button btn btn-sm btn-primary mb-sm-0 mr-sm-1"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="nav-link external-link-vp text-white" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#accessibility-modal" href="#accessibility-modal" aria-label="Доступность">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="nav-link external-link-vp text-white"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="https://www.eesti.ee/ru" target="_blank" class="nav-link" rel="noopener">Eesti.ee</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="nav-link"]`

*... and 6 more failures for this rule*

- HTML: `<a href="/download_all_files/27" target="_blank" aria-label="Failide allalaadimine ja vaatamine" class="ml-auto text-right d-flex align-items-center w-fit justify-content-end js-documents-download" rel="noopener">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="ml-auto text-right d-flex align-items-center w-fit justify-content-end js-documents-download"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R18: ARIA states are consistent with element semantics](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r18)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is prohibited for the element on which it is specified

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<a class="nav-link dropdown-toggle" id="header-menu-dropdown" href="#" data-toggle="dropdown" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">               Ministeeriumid             </a>`
- XPath: `/a[@id="header-menu-dropdown"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R53: Headings follow a logical hierarchy](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r53)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The heading skips one or more levels
- HTML: `<h4>Püsi kursis</h4>`
- XPath: `/h4`

#### Rule: [SIA-R56: Landmarks with the same role are distinguishable](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r56)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Some `navigation` have the same name.

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 5.39:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R77](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r77)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The cell is not assigned to any header cell
- HTML: `<td class=" text-center no-wrap-vp doc-item-url">...</td>`
- XPath: `/td[@class=" text-center no-wrap-vp doc-item-url"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R87: First focusable element is a skip link](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r87)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The first tabbable element in the document is not a semantic link

### https://valitsus.ee/strateegia-eesti-2035-arengukavad-ja-planeering/strateegilised-arengudokumendid

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button type="button" class="eu-cookie-compliance-select-categories-button btn btn-outline-light btn-sm mr-2" tabindex="0">Valin ise</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="eu-cookie-compliance-select-categories-button btn btn-outline-light btn-sm mr-2"]`

- Message: Target has insufficient size

- XPath: `/button[@class="agree-necessary btn btn-outline-light btn-sm mr-2"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button type="button" class="agree-button btn btn-sm btn-primary mb-sm-0 mr-sm-1" tabindex="0">Luban kõik</button>`

- XPath: `/a[@class="nav-link external-link-vp text-white"]`

- Message: Target has insufficient size

- XPath: `/a[@class="nav-link"]`

- HTML: `<a class="nav-link external-link-vp text-white" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#accessibility-modal" href="#accessibility-modal" aria-label="Juurdepääsetavus">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="nav-link external-link-vp text-white"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="https://www.eesti.ee/et" target="_blank" class="nav-link" rel="noopener">Eesti.ee</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="nav-link"]`

- Message: Some `navigation` have the same name.

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 5.39:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R68: Accessible name contains the visible label text](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r68)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element owns no elements as required by its semantic role
- HTML: `<ul class="list-unstyled list-vp list-tick-vp"> </ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@class="list-unstyled list-vp list-tick-vp"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R87: First focusable element is a skip link](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r87)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The first tabbable element in the document is not a semantic link

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button type="button" class="eu-cookie-compliance-select-categories-button btn btn-outline-light btn-sm mr-2" tabindex="0">Выбрать самому</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="eu-cookie-compliance-select-categories-button btn btn-outline-light btn-sm mr-2"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button type="button" class="agree-necessary btn btn-outline-light btn-sm mr-2" tabindex="0">Разрешить необходимые</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="agree-necessary btn btn-outline-light btn-sm mr-2"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button type="button" class="agree-button btn btn-sm btn-primary mb-sm-0 mr-sm-1" tabindex="0">Разрешить все</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="agree-button btn btn-sm btn-primary mb-sm-0 mr-sm-1"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="nav-link external-link-vp text-white" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#accessibility-modal" href="#accessibility-modal" aria-label="Доступность">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="nav-link external-link-vp text-white"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="https://www.eesti.ee/ru" target="_blank" class="nav-link" rel="noopener">Eesti.ee</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="nav-link"]`

*... and 6 more failures for this rule*

**Failure 1:**

- XPath: `/a[@class="nav-link"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

- HTML: `<a class="nav-link dropdown-toggle" id="header-menu-dropdown" href="#" data-toggle="dropdown" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">               Ministeeriumid             </a>`
- XPath: `/a[@id="header-menu-dropdown"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R53: Headings follow a logical hierarchy](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r53)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The heading skips one or more levels
- HTML: `<h5>Töö- ja teenistuskäik</h5>`
- XPath: `/h5`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The heading skips one or more levels
- HTML: `<h4>Püsi kursis</h4>`
- XPath: `/h4`

#### Rule: [SIA-R56: Landmarks with the same role are distinguishable](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r56)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Some `navigation` have the same name.

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 5.39:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R77](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r77)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The cell is not assigned to any header cell
- HTML: `<td class=" text-center no-wrap-vp doc-item-url">...</td>`
- XPath: `/td[@class=" text-center no-wrap-vp doc-item-url"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R87: First focusable element is a skip link](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r87)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The first tabbable element in the document is not a semantic link

### https://valitsus.ee/ru/kabinet-ministrov/ministr-regionalnogo-razvitiya-i-selskogo-khozyaystva-khendrik-yokhannes-terras

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button type="button" class="eu-cookie-compliance-select-categories-button btn btn-outline-light btn-sm mr-2" tabindex="0">Выбрать самому</button>`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button type="button" class="agree-button btn btn-sm btn-primary mb-sm-0 mr-sm-1" tabindex="0">Разрешить все</button>`

- XPath: `/a[@class="nav-link"]`

- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 5.39:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The first tabbable element in the document is not a semantic link

### https://valitsus.ee/strateegia-eesti-2035-arengukavad-ja-planeering/strateegilised-arengudokumendid/poliitika

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button type="button" class="eu-cookie-compliance-select-categories-button btn btn-outline-light btn-sm mr-2" tabindex="0">Valin ise</button>`

- HTML: `<button type="button" class="agree-button btn btn-sm btn-primary mb-sm-0 mr-sm-1" tabindex="0">Luban kõik</button>`

- XPath: `/a[@class="nav-link external-link-vp text-white"]`

- Message: Target has insufficient size

- XPath: `/a[@class="nav-link"]`

- HTML: `<button type="button" class="eu-cookie-compliance-select-categories-button btn btn-outline-light btn-sm mr-2" tabindex="0">Manage cookies</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="eu-cookie-compliance-select-categories-button btn btn-outline-light btn-sm mr-2"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button type="button" class="agree-necessary btn btn-outline-light btn-sm mr-2" tabindex="0">Allow only necessary</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="agree-necessary btn btn-outline-light btn-sm mr-2"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button type="button" class="agree-button btn btn-sm btn-primary mb-sm-0 mr-sm-1" tabindex="0">Allow all</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="agree-button btn btn-sm btn-primary mb-sm-0 mr-sm-1"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="nav-link external-link-vp text-white" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#accessibility-modal" href="#accessibility-modal" aria-label="Accessibility">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="nav-link external-link-vp text-white"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="https://www.eesti.ee/et/" target="_blank" class="nav-link" rel="noopener">Eesti.ee</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="nav-link"]`

*... and 10 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R18: ARIA states are consistent with element semantics](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r18)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is prohibited for the element on which it is specified

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<a class="nav-link dropdown-toggle" id="header-menu-dropdown" href="#" data-toggle="dropdown" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">               Ministries             </a>`
- XPath: `/a[@id="header-menu-dropdown"]`

- HTML: `<h3>We will ensure a viable cultural space</h3>`
- XPath: `/h3`

- Message: The heading skips one or more levels
- HTML: `<h4>Follow updates</h4>`
- XPath: `/h4`

- Message: Some `navigation` have the same name.

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 5.39:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The first tabbable element in the document is not a semantic link

## Detailed Failure Information (axe)

### https://valitsus.ee/

#### Rule: [aria-allowed-attr](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-allowed-attr?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements must only use supported ARIA attributes
- HTML: `<span class="nav-link dropdown-toggle is-active" id="header-language-dropdown" data-toggle="dropdown" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false" tabindex="0">         EST       </span>`
- XPath: `#header-language-dropdown`

- XPath: `.focusable`

- XPath: `.mt-4.container-body-md-vp[data-aos="fade-up"]:nth-child(1) > .z-index-1.paragraph--type--horizontal-split.position-relative > .row-large-gutters-vp.aos-init[data-aos="fade-up"] > .col-xl-4.col-lg-6 > .paragraph--view-mode--view-mode-selector.paragraph--type--text-section.paragraph > .field--name-field-text-section-content.mb-3.field--type-text-long > h3`

#### Rule: [landmark-unique](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/landmark-unique?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

- XPath: `.col-md-4.col-sm-6:nth-child(1) > h4`

#### Rule: [landmark-unique](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/landmark-unique?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Landmarks should have a unique role or role/label/title (i.e. accessible name) combination
- HTML: `<nav class="navbar navbar-expand-md navbar-dark navbar-top-vp w-100">`
- XPath: `#block-headerblock > .navbar-expand-md.navbar-top-vp.navbar-dark`

#### Rule: [region](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/region?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<a href="#main-content" class="visually-hidden focusable skip-link">       Skip to main content     </a>`
- XPath: `.focusable`

### https://valitsus.ee/en/node/31

#### Rule: [aria-allowed-attr](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-allowed-attr?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements must only use supported ARIA attributes
- HTML: `<span class="nav-link dropdown-toggle is-active" id="header-language-dropdown" data-toggle="dropdown" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false" tabindex="0">         ENG       </span>`
- XPath: `#header-language-dropdown`

#### Rule: [empty-table-header](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/empty-table-header?application=playwright)
**Impact**: minor

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Table header text should not be empty
- HTML: `<th class="text-center no-wrap-vp doc-item-url sorting_disabled" rowspan="1" colspan="1" aria-label="Files download and view"></th>`
- XPath: `#DataTables_Table_0 > thead > tr > .sorting_disabled`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Table header text should not be empty
- HTML: `<th class="text-center no-wrap-vp doc-item-url sorting_disabled" rowspan="1" colspan="1" aria-label="Files download and view"></th>`
- XPath: `#DataTables_Table_1 > thead > tr > .sorting_disabled`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Table header text should not be empty
- HTML: `<th class="text-center no-wrap-vp doc-item-url sorting_disabled" rowspan="1" colspan="1" aria-label="Files download and view"></th>`
- XPath: `#DataTables_Table_2 > thead > tr > .sorting_disabled`

#### Rule: [heading-order](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/heading-order?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Heading levels should only increase by one
- HTML: `<h4>Follow updates</h4>`
- XPath: `.col-md-4.col-sm-6:nth-child(1) > h4`

#### Rule: [landmark-unique](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/landmark-unique?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Landmarks should have a unique role or role/label/title (i.e. accessible name) combination
- HTML: `<nav class="navbar navbar-expand-md navbar-dark navbar-top-vp w-100">`
- XPath: `#block-headerblock > .navbar-expand-md.navbar-top-vp.navbar-dark`

#### Rule: [region](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/region?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<a href="#main-content" class="visually-hidden focusable skip-link">       Skip to main content     </a>`
